info:Super Room (Double bed)

info:12 Reviews
rating:4.6
posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:The hotel is in a good location and has a high floor, but not all of the buildings are hotels, and some of them are rented out to other businesses. Fortunately, you can swipe your card to go upstairs, so the security is still OK!
The hotel may be old, and the facilities are a bit outdated, but the high floor has a good view! The super-large bed is enough for a family of three, and the room is also large and spacious. The sanitation is not very careful. There is a poker box under our bed. It has its own charging cable and 3 interfaces, which is perfect. There is also a USB charging port, but the TV has no smart function, and you can't cast the screen with your phone, you can only watch TV programs!
I temporarily upgraded to a riverside super-large bed room. The hotel gave 3 fruit and coffee coupons that can be exchanged for coffee at the Starbucks service point in the lobby. The service is very good! The staff at the coffee bar are also very enthusiastic and have a good attitude...
But Jiangyin is not a tourist city, and there are not many guests. Most of them come to attend banquets!

msg:During the Qingming Festival, I took the elderly and children back to my grandfather's hometown. I chose the Wyndham by the river. The river view king room has a good view, and the elderly feel great living there. The hotel is only a 15-minute drive from Ebizui Park, which is very convenient.
Special thanks to Lucy at the front desk, the service is kind and patient. I booked a river view room and a twin room. When checking in, I told her that I wanted to be on the same floor. Lucy helped us check the room situation and finally found a suitable floor. The two rooms are very close, and it is very convenient for children to go back and forth between the two rooms.
Lucy is also very attentive. It was my husband's birthday on the day of check-in. Lucy and her colleagues brought cakes, fruit baskets and sparkling wine to the room, which really made us feel the hotel's thoughtfulness!
When I checked out the next day, the hotel also gave me water chestnut cakes and drinks, which is really very hospitable! I will stay here again when I come back!

name:Tâ€aâ€oâ€yâ€uâ€aâ€nâ€jâ€iâ€aâ€nâ€gâ€wâ€eâ€i
info:Superior Room (Double bed)
info:Stayed in May 2023

info:105 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 19, 2023
msg:Jiangyin Changsheng Wyndham Hotel is a high-end hotel located in Jiangyin City, Jiangsu Province. I stayed at this hotel last month and was very satisfied with my stay. Here is my review:

First of all, the location of the hotel is very good. It is located in the center of Jiangyin, very close to the railway station and the airport. There are many shopping centers, restaurants and attractions within a few minutes' walk of the hotel, and there are many business districts and office buildings around for you to choose from.

Second, the hotel rooms are very spacious and comfortable. I live in a deluxe room, the room area is about 30 square meters, the decoration style is modern and simple, full of artistic a**osphere. The rooms are fully equipped, including air conditioning, TV, refrigerator, safe, free Wi-Fi, etc., making me feel very comfortable and convenient. In addition, the room has a balcony with a beautiful view of the city.

Third, the service of the hotel is excellent. The receptionists are very friendly and welcoming, they do their best to meet the needs of the guests. The hotel also has a 24-hour front desk service, so I can get help and support at any time. In addition, the hotel also provides laundry, taxi and other services to make life more convenient for guests.

Finally, the hotel's catering is also excellent. There is a large restaurant in the hotel, which provides a variety of cuisines, including Chinese food, Western food and Japanese food. I tried some dishes and they were all delicious. The hotel also has a coffee shop and a bar for guests' leisure and entertainment.

In short, Jiangyin Changsheng Wyndham Hotel is an excellent hotel, with its superior location, spacious and comfortable rooms, thoughtful and meticulous service, and rich and varied restaurants. If you have a chance to come to Jiangyin City, I strongly recommend you to stay in this hotel.
